2024-05-21 08:04:02====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'BDA242D4-DFC4-13A2-E054-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            And a.事件id = '66B74E9C-2F1D-4A5E-A503-CF1D2343052F'
                            And a.组序号 in (29)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 09:13:50====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='18EC0CA8-C74E-2315-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='18EC0CA8-C74E-2315-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
2024-05-21 09:13:50====>获取诊断信息:Select B.主诉 As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+)
                               And A.id='18EC0CA8-C74E-2315-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                               And Rownum<2
                            Union All
                            Select Distinct '' As chiefCompliant,C.问题名称 As diagName,C.问题编码 As diagCode
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,个人问题列表 C
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id  And A.Id=C.服务记录id(+) And C.记录性质=2 
                               And A.id='18EC0CA8-C74E-2315-E064-9CDC71ADEEF6'
                               And Rownum<2

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b54bee96-db75-4d19-8595-aeea6f96f4da'
                            And a.事件id = '6B952570-771B-466D-A1B8-0BAD0D7B3C4F'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 09:44:43====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b54bee96-db75-4d19-8595-aeea6f96f4da'
                            And a.事件id = '6B952570-771B-466D-A1B8-0BAD0D7B3C4F'
                            And a.组序号 in (17)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 11:41:36====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'D192B87A-33A2-24FA-E054-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.事件id = 'D3BB36E7-421D-44EF-AABF-E47F40C4D258'
                            And a.组序号 in (13)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 11:44:32====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'D192B87A-33A2-24FA-E054-9CDC71ADEB60'
                            And a.事件id = 'D3BB36E7-421D-44EF-AABF-E47F40C4D258'
                            And a.组序号 in (16)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 14:42:26====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'

2024-05-21 14:42:27====>获取就诊信息:Select Decode(B.急诊,1,'2','1') As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,'' As wardCode,'' As wardName,'' As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人挂号记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D
                             Where A.Id=B.记录id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id
                               And A.id='B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'
                            Union All
                            Select '3' As visitTypeCode,A.ID As visitNo,to_char(A.开始时间,'yyyymmdd') As visitDate,
                                   C.编码 As deptCode,C.简称 As deptName,E.编码 As wardCode,E.简称 As wardName,B.床号 As bedNo,
                                   D.编码 As doctorId,D.姓名 As doctorName,D.身份证号 As doctorIdentityNo
                              From 服务活动记录 A,个人入院记录 B,部门 C,医护人员 D,部门 E
                             Where A.Id=B.事件id And A.科室id=C.资源id And A.服务人id=D.资源id And B.病房id=E.资源id(+)
                               And A.id='B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'

                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b20716dc-9795-4ea2-876a-85aa54820f0d'
                            And a.事件id = 'B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'
                            And a.组序号 in (15)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno

2024-05-21 14:42:29====>获取project_list:select sno,project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,min(project_charge_code) as project_charge_code,study_project_code,sum(project_price) as project_price from 
                        (Select Distinct A.子序号 As sno, c.名称     As project_name,
                                nvl(a.标本部位,'-') As study_body_part,
                                    to_char(a.医嘱附注.getclobval()) As study_method,
                                a.操作类型 As modality,
                                nvl(f.国家代码,'-') As project_charge_code,
                                Decode(a.标本部位,Null,c.id,c.id||'-'||c.部位编码) As study_project_code,
                                nvl(B.单价,0) As project_price
                           From 个人医嘱记录 A,
                                个人医嘱计价 B,
                                保险项目对应 F,
                                (select Distinct C.id,C.名称,h.编码 as 部位编码,h.名称 as 部位
                                   from 诊疗项目目录 C,诊疗项目部位 g,诊疗检查部位 h
                                  where c.id=g.项目id(+) and g.类型=h.类型(+) and g.部位=h.名称(+) And g.分组=H.分组(+)) C
                            Where a.机构id = '4480c78d-c3dd-4873-a0a8-d936963abf75'
                            And a.个人id = 'b20716dc-9795-4ea2-876a-85aa54820f0d'
                            And a.事件id = 'B2C8F172-1E63-434B-9B3E-CF11DAE1C207'
                            And a.组序号 in (17)
                            And B.收费项目id=F.收费id(+)
                            And a.Id = b.医嘱id(+)
                            And a.诊疗项目id = c.Id
                            And (a.标本部位=c.部位 or a.标本部位 Is Null))
                        group By sno, project_name,study_body_part,study_method,modality,study_project_code
                        Order By sno
